LATE DAILY MASS In Sacred Heart Church at 9:30, 10:30, and 11:30 A.M., Monday through Saturday. Also, Monday through Friday at 5:10 P.M. 
HOLY COMMUNION Those who are unable to attend Mass are reminded that Holy Communion is distributed until 9:20 A.M. every morning, except Sundays and Holy Days, in Dillon, Howard, Cavanaugh, and Stanford-Keenan chapels, and between the late daily Masses in Sacred 
Heart Church. MORNING CONFESSIONS 
Confessions are heard in the morning during the Masses in all the hall chapels; until 
9:20 A.M. in Dillon, Howard, Cavanaugh, and Stanford-Keenan chapels; and during and between the late daily Masses in Sacred Heart Church. Also, during Sunday Masses in Sacred Heait Church and in Stanford-Keenan chapel. 
EVENING CONFESSIONS Confessions aie heard during the evening Mass in Sacred Heart Church; in Dillon between 6:30 and 10:00 P.M.; in Howard and Cavanaugh between 7:00 and 9:30 P.M.; and in Stanford-Keenan between 6:30 and 9:30 P.M.; and on Saturday evening in Sacred Heart Church between 6:00 and 8:30 P. M.
